# 轻小说 2014~2017 NPM、PYPI、DockerHub 备份

## 爱的禁行式 - 本谷有希子 - 20140814


### Docker

```
docker pull apachecn0/ai-de-jinxing-shi-bengu-you-xizi-20140814
docker run -tid -p <port>:80 apachecn0/ai-de-jinxing-shi-bengu-you-xizi-20140814
# 访问 http://localhost:{port} 查看文档
```

### PYPI

```
pip install ai-de-jinxing-shi-bengu-you-xizi-20140814
ai-de-jinxing-shi-bengu-you-xizi-20140814 <port>
# 访问 http://localhost:{port} 查看文档
```

### NPM

```
npm install -g ai-de-jinxing-shi-bengu-you-xizi-erlingyisilingbayisi
ai-de-jinxing-shi-bengu-you-xizi-erlingyisilingbayisi <port>
# 访问 http://localhost:{port} 查看文档
```

```
docker pull apachecn0/wuzhi-youling-kuiguan-nan-20140106
docker run -tid -p <port>:80 apachecn0/wuzhi-youling-kuiguan-nan-20140106
# 访问 http://localhost:{port} 查看文档
```

### PYPI

```
pip install wuzhi-youling-kuiguan-nan-20140106
wuzhi-youling-kuiguan-nan-20140106 <port>
# 访问 http://localhost:{port} 查看文档
```

### NPM

```
npm install -g wuzhi-youling-kuiguan-nan-erlingyisilingyilingliu
wuzhi-youling-kuiguan-nan-erlingyisilingyilingliu <port>
# 访问 http://localhost:{port} 查看文档
```
